The lobby is very beautiful and the rooms are very comfortable, but the design is not very reasonable. There is an unparalleled sea view outside the window, but most of the view is blocked by the large stone exterior wall and the thick and high-quality door.

The children's paradise is not big, but it is enough for preschoolers to play, and the children also have fun in the daily handicraft classes. There are some paid items in the children's park. We took the go-kart family car. We forgot whether it was 78 or 88. It was really fun, but the time was too short and only allowed you three laps. Of course, you can play as many laps as you want if you continue to pay. , so this is a problem with our wallets, not the kart itself. The claw machine is only 3 to 5 yuan a time, the carousel is 10 yuan a time, and there are two small rocking cars outside the door for only 2 yuan a time. It's really a good price. The water play area has been closed since November. There is a small outdoor playground next to it. The maintenance is average. Two swings were broken and no one repaired it.

The hotel has two buildings. We stayed in Xihai. The lobby is very tall. The brochure said that the glass roof was hand-made in Italy. The stone for the exterior wall was sourced from the same mine as the Palace of Versailles. It felt a bit strange. Feel. The swimming pool, gym and children's craft room are also in this building. The children's playground is in the Ruihai building, and the lobby is a bit crude.

The European-style town next to it also has hotels according to the Internet, but it is too deserted and has nothing, and it is estimated that no one lives there. Next to it is the seaside promenade and beach. It gets a bit sunny during the day, but it is really pleasant to take a walk and enjoy the sea breeze at night.
